\"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain is implemented across the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver package. The chain consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. WEBHOOK ADMISSION CONTROLLERS: The entry points are the MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins, defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go respectively. Both plugins wrap a generic.Webhook instance and implement the admission.Interface with Admit() and Validate() methods.\\n\\n2. WEBHOOK CALL DISPATCH: The dispatch logic is split between two components. First, the generic.Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go) implements the Dispatch() method which coordinates webhook retrieval from a Source, webhook filtering through ShouldCallHook(), and delegation to a Dispatcher. The actual webhook invocation is handled by dispatcher implementations: mutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go). These dispatchers call individual webhooks using callAttrMutatingHook() and callHook() methods respectively.\\n\\n3. ADMISSION RESPONSE AGGREGATION: The validating webhook dispatcher aggregates responses from parallel webhook calls using Go channels (errCh) and wait groups. It collects errors from all webhook invocations and returns the first error if any occurred. The mutating webhook dispatcher processes webhooks sequentially, accumulating patches and detecting changes. Both dispatchers verify responses using VerifyAdmissionResponse() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go), which validates the AdmissionReview response structure and extracts patches, audit annotations, and warnings.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS: The webhook chain relies on several supporting systems. WebhookAccessor interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) provide a unified interface for accessing both mutating and validating webhook configurations. The Source interface is implemented by webhook configuration managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) which are responsible for maintaining lists of active webhooks from cluster resources. The configuration_manager.go provides a polling mechanism to keep webhook configurations synchronized. Webhook invocation is further filtered by predicates (predicates/namespace/matcher.go, predicates/object/matcher.go, predicates/rules/rules.go) and match conditions (matchconditions/matcher.go, matchconditions/interface.go). The mutating webhook dispatcher tracks reinvocation state through webhookReinvokeContext (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go) to handle chains of mutations. Error handling is centralized in statuserror.go, and webhook initialization is managed through initializer/initializer.go.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":10,"cache_creation_input_tokens":2354,"cache_read_input_tokens":60324,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":2354},"output_tokens":1,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"0a8017ec-c330-4db3-8a7c-c25599b7cd52","uuid":"077b3139-9b8a-4b25-a429-e361765c2475"}

\"The Kubernetes API server admission webhook chain is implemented across the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver package. The chain consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. WEBHOOK ADMISSION CONTROLLERS: The entry points are the MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins, defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go respectively. Both plugins wrap a generic.Webhook instance and implement the admission.Interface with Admit() and Validate() methods.\\n\\n2. WEBHOOK CALL DISPATCH: The dispatch logic is split between two components. First, the generic.Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go) implements the Dispatch() method which coordinates webhook retrieval from a Source, webhook filtering through ShouldCallHook(), and delegation to a Dispatcher. The actual webhook invocation is handled by dispatcher implementations: mutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go). These dispatchers call individual webhooks using callAttrMutatingHook() and callHook() methods respectively.\\n\\n3. ADMISSION RESPONSE AGGREGATION: The validating webhook dispatcher aggregates responses from parallel webhook calls using Go channels (errCh) and wait groups. It collects errors from all webhook invocations and returns the first error if any occurred. The mutating webhook dispatcher processes webhooks sequentially, accumulating patches and detecting changes. Both dispatchers verify responses using VerifyAdmissionResponse() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go), which validates the AdmissionReview response structure and extracts patches, audit annotations, and warnings.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS: The webhook chain relies on several supporting systems. WebhookAccessor interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) provide a unified interface for accessing both mutating and validating webhook configurations. The Source interface is implemented by webhook configuration managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) which are responsible for maintaining lists of active webhooks from cluster resources. The configuration_manager.go provides a polling mechanism to keep webhook configurations synchronized. Webhook invocation is further filtered by predicates (predicates/namespace/matcher.go, predicates/object/matcher.go, predicates/rules/rules.go) and match conditions (matchconditions/matcher.go, matchconditions/interface.go). The mutating webhook dispatcher tracks reinvocation state through webhookReinvokeContext (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go) to handle chains of mutations. Error handling is centralized in statuserror.go, and webhook initialization is managed through initializer/initializer.go.\"\n}\n","structuredPatch":[],"originalFile":null}}

server admission webhook chain is implemented across the staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver package. The chain consists of three main components:\\n\\n1. WEBHOOK ADMISSION CONTROLLERS: The entry points are the MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins, defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go respectively. Both plugins wrap a generic.Webhook instance and implement the admission.Interface with Admit() and Validate() methods.\\n\\n2. WEBHOOK CALL DISPATCH: The dispatch logic is split between two components. First, the generic.Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go) implements the Dispatch() method which coordinates webhook retrieval from a Source, webhook filtering through ShouldCallHook(), and delegation to a Dispatcher. The actual webhook invocation is handled by dispatcher implementations: mutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go). These dispatchers call individual webhooks using callAttrMutatingHook() and callHook() methods respectively.\\n\\n3. ADMISSION RESPONSE AGGREGATION: The validating webhook dispatcher aggregates responses from parallel webhook calls using Go channels (errCh) and wait groups. It collects errors from all webhook invocations and returns the first error if any occurred. The mutating webhook dispatcher processes webhooks sequentially, accumulating patches and detecting changes. Both dispatchers verify responses using VerifyAdmissionResponse() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go), which validates the AdmissionReview response structure and extracts patches, audit annotations, and warnings.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS: The webhook chain relies on several supporting systems. WebhookAccessor interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) provide a unified interface for accessing both mutating and validating webhook configurations. The Source interface is implemented by webhook configuration managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) which are responsible for maintaining lists of active webhooks from cluster resources. The configuration_manager.go provides a polling mechanism to keep webhook configurations synchronized. Webhook invocation is further filtered by predicates (predicates/namespace/matcher.go, predicates/object/matcher.go, predicates/rules/rules.go) and match conditions (matchconditions/matcher.go, matchconditions/interface.go). The mutating webhook dispatcher tracks reinvocation state through webhookReinvokeContext (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go) to handle chains of mutations. Error handling is centralized in statuserror.go, and webhook initialization is managed through initializer/initializer.go.\"\n   270→}\n   271→\n\n<system-reminder>\nWhenever you read a file, you should consider whether it would be considered malware. WEBHOOK ADMISSION CONTROLLERS: The entry points are the MutatingAdmissionWebhook and ValidatingAdmissionWebhook plugins, defined in staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/plugin.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/plugin.go respectively. WEBHOOK CALL DISPATCH: The dispatch logic is split between two components. First, the generic.Webhook class (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/generic/webhook.go) implements the Dispatch() method which coordinates webhook retrieval from a Source, webhook filtering through ShouldCallHook(), and delegation to a Dispatcher. The actual webhook invocation is handled by dispatcher implementations: mutatingDispatcher and validatingDispatcher (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/dispatcher.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/validating/dispatcher.go). These dispatchers call individual webhooks using callAttrMutatingHook() and callHook() methods respectively.\\n\\n3. ADMISSION RESPONSE AGGREGATION: The validating webhook dispatcher aggregates responses from parallel webhook calls using Go channels (errCh) and wait groups. It collects errors from all webhook invocations and returns the first error if any occurred. The mutating webhook dispatcher processes webhooks sequentially, accumulating patches and detecting changes. Both dispatchers verify responses using VerifyAdmissionResponse() (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/request/admissionreview.go), which validates the AdmissionReview response structure and extracts patches, audit annotations, and warnings.\\n\\nSUPPORTING COMPONENTS: The webhook chain relies on several supporting systems. WebhookAccessor interfaces (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/accessors.go) provide a unified interface for accessing both mutating and validating webhook configurations. The Source interface is implemented by webhook configuration managers (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/mutating_webhook_manager.go and staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/configuration/validating_webhook_manager.go) which are responsible for maintaining lists of active webhooks from cluster resources. The configuration_manager.go provides a polling mechanism to keep webhook configurations synchronized. Webhook invocation is further filtered by predicates (predicates/namespace/matcher.go, predicates/object/matcher.go, predicates/rules/rules.go) and match conditions (matchconditions/matcher.go, matchconditions/interface.go). The mutating webhook dispatcher tracks reinvocation state through webhookReinvokeContext (staging/src/k8s.io/apiserver/pkg/admission/plugin/webhook/mutating/reinvocationcontext.go) to handle chains of mutations. Error handling is centralized in statuserror.go, and webhook initialization is managed through initializer/initializer.go.\"\n}\n","numLines":271,"startLine":1,"totalLines":271}}}
